{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:06:21.460" end="01:06:27.460" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And what was interesting is not coming from us on this ed tech council, but as said back to us by the consultants, it said, gee, what's really important at MIT is the integration of research and education.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}结果有趣的结论并不是来自我们教育技术委员会，而是由顾问们反馈给我们的， 他们说，哎，MIT 真正重要的是研究与教育的融合。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:06:42.430" end="01:06:43.270" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And now what's that say?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这意味着什么呢？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:06:43.270" end="01:06:46.170" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}That says if you're thinking about distance learning in this sense, if somehow that is just curriculum material and it's not infused with the notion of research, that's kind of not an MIT education.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这意味着，如果你从这个角度思考远程教育，如果它只是讲课程材料，而没有融入研究的理念，那它就不算是 MIT 式的教育。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:06:59.450" end="01:07:02.630" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So that one kind of fundamental they heard.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这是他们听到的一个基本点。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:02.630" end="01:07:04.470" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Another one they heard which this notion of an integrated faculty.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}他们听到的另一个基本点是一体化教师队伍的概念。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:06.770" end="01:07:09.780" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So MIT, unlike lots of other places, has this notion of one faculty.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}MIT 与许多其他地方不同，它有一个 “统一的教师队伍”的概念。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:11.020" end="01:07:14.470" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We don't have graduate faculty or we don't have teaching faculty and research faculty.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们没有研究生导师，也没有教学教职与研究教职之分。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:16.120" end="01:07:17.800" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We have faculty.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们就只有教职员工。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:17.800" end="01:07:19.470" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And there's the sense if you're on the faculty, you're supposed to do all of these things.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}并且有一种观念是，如果你在教师团队中， 你就应该承担所有这些职责。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:21.730" end="01:07:27.610" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So there's this notion of if we really went and like oh, the Harvard Extension School, had a whole bunch of people who are not actual Harvard faculty who were teaching this thing, ahh, that's not the sort of thing MIT does.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以我们的想法是，如果我们真的像哈佛大学继续教育学院（Harvard Extension School）那样， 让一大批不是真正的哈佛教师的人来讲课， 啊，那可不是 MIT 的做法。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:38.610" end="01:07:42.080" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So there were a bunch of principles like that.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}于是就有了一系列这样的原则。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:42.080" end="01:07:45.410" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And eventually we were sort of saying as MIT goes forward, do we think about expanding to new communities?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}最终我们在讨论的是，随着 MIT 向前发展， 我们是否要考虑扩展到新的群体？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:07:48.830" end="01:07:55.280" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Right now we think of our potential student body as the top whatever it is, two percent, three percent of students in the world.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}目前我们把潜在学生群体定义为排名顶尖， 大概是全球排名前 2% 或 3% 的学生。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:08:05.200" end="01:08:08.590" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Should we be the top 10 percent?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们是否应该面向前 10%？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:08:08.590" end="01:08:13.490" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So there was this notion of who we actually talk to?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}进而有了这样的想法：我们究竟要与谁对话？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:08:13.490" end="01:08:16.819" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And we kind of strategically said we actually want to stay with the communities of people that we know.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}从战略上我们大概说，我们实际上想留在我们所熟悉的人组成的社群里。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:08:20.000" end="01:08:25.170" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And we want to stay with an MIT of kind of style thing.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}并且我们希望保持一种 MIT 的风格。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:08:25.170" end="01:08:29.300" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And that morphed into a thing that said we really want to change the dynamic of how a student interacts with MIT to something that can be lifelong.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}事情演变成，我们想要的是改变学生与 MIT 互动的模式，使其成为一种终身的关系。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:08:39.270" end="01:08:42.529" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So there was this idea that right now you graduate MIT, and what it means basically means to be an alum is that every year the Institute sends you requests for money.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以就有了这样一个想法，现在你从 MIT 毕业成为校友，基本上只意味着学院每年会向你发出捐款请求。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:08:50.090" end="01:08:54.240" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And we're saying shouldn't there be a different kind of thing with that where you can participate in this community intellectually for a long time?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们说，难道不应该有另一种形式吗，让你可以在智识上长期参与到这个社区中？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:08:58.970" end="01:09:00.853" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So that was one of these things called lifelong education.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以那就是一种所谓的 “终身教育”（lifelong education）的东西。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:09:02.103" end="01:09:04.729" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And so out of that strategic thing, there came another thing, saying well, we kind of decided on that as the direction.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}于是，在那一轮战略规划之后，产生了另一个想法，说，好，我们大致已经决定了这个方向。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:09:13.149" end="01:09:16.149" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Let's mush out this lifelong learning thing.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们来把这个终身学习的概念具体化。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:09:16.149" end="01:09:17.229" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Let's figure out what it is.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们来搞明白它到底是什么。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:09:17.229" end="01:09:19.460" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We actually did another consulting engagement with Booz Allen, who came in as very analytical, saying is this going to work?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们实际上请来了 Booz Allen 做另一轮咨询，他们非常分析性地来， 讨论“这行得通吗？”{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:09:25.149" end="01:09:30.630" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And basically after long drawn-out things and analyses and talking to possible clients and competitors and offices at MIT about everything, they found it wasn't going to work.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后基本上在经过了漫长的过程，各种分析， 与潜在客户、竞争对手以及 MIT 内部各办公室进行方方面面的沟通之后，他们发现行不通。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:09:38.520" end="01:09:44.040" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So they called in one of their spreadsheet ninjas, who made this giant thing with every possible parameter you could imagine, what are the production values, how long is the course, what's the client thing.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}于是他们找来了他们的一位电子表格高手， 做了一个巨大的东西，包含了你能想象到的每一个可能的参数，产品价值有哪些、 课程多长、客户情况如何。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:09:52.350" end="01:09:56.600" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And basically it turned out that, I forget, if you've got 20,000 doing a course, you could kind of a break-even, maybe.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}结果基本上是，我忘了，如果你有两万人上一门课，你或许能勉强收支平衡，大概。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:05.740" end="01:10:08.570" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So this whole committee was actually pretty-- oh my god, what are we going to do?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}于是整个委员会当时都相当——老天爷， 我们咋办啊？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:11.620" end="01:10:13.430" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And finally, I think it was Dick Yue, there's some famous story--{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}最后，我想应该是 Dick Yue， 有个很著名的故事——{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:14.600" end="01:10:15.590" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}I don't know if you talked to him.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我不知道你有没有和他聊过。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:15.590" end="01:10:17.480" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}There's this famous story about he was exercising or something.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}有个著名的故事说，他当时在锻炼身体还是什么。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:19.490" end="01:10:21.550" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And it sort of came to him about well, why don't we take this stuff and give it away.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后他突然灵光一现，诶，我们为什么不把这些东西直接免费送人呢。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:23.780" end="01:10:25.520" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And that sounds like a crazy idea.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这听起来是个疯狂的想法。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:25.520" end="01:10:28.270" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But then you sort of think well you know, if we're not going to make money charging alumni and other people to do this, maybe we can get foundations to pay for this.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但你接着会想到，好吧， 如果我们无法通过向校友和其他人收费来赚钱，也许我们可以让基金会来买单。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:36.340" end="01:10:39.900" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So it wasn't a totally crazy idea.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以这也不完全是个疯狂的想法。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:39.900" end="01:10:46.100" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And then at the end of the summer what happened was the committee produced this report.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}那年夏末，委员会最终提交了一份报告。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:49.410" end="01:10:51.630" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So that was the other thing that Dick did.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}那是 Dick 做的另一件事。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:51.630" end="01:10:53.320" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}MIT believes in data.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}MIT 崇尚数据。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:10:53.320" end="01:10:56.210" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And he did this amazing thing, which is whenever the consultants would do anything, they'd interview somebody, and he'd sort of xerox the sheet.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}他做了一件非常厉害的事情，就是每当顾问做什么事情时，比如要访谈某人， 他就会把那张纸复印下来。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:01.020" end="01:11:03.210" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And he put it in this big notebook.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后把它们装进一个大笔记本里。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:03.210" end="01:11:07.790" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And he had a notebook which was literally this high.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}他那个笔记本，真有这么高。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:07.790" end="01:11:10.680" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And when he'd come in to make a presentation, he'd put the notebook on the desk, saying the committee has done this research for its conclusions.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}当他来做报告时，他会把笔记本往桌上一放，说委员会做了这项研究， 得出了这些结论。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:16.300" end="01:11:19.430" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And nobody would dare challenge him on that, despite the fact that nothing in the notebook was relevant to what he was saying.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}没人敢质疑他，尽管笔记本里实际上没有一样和他说的事情有关系。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:22.132" end="01:11:23.710" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It was just a great, great ploy.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这真是个非常非常妙的策略。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:23.710" end="01:11:26.210" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But it's again, engineer's culture.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但这也再次体现了工程师文化。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:26.210" end="01:11:28.810" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We like data.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们喜欢数据。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:28.810" end="01:11:33.300" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But the committee's report was this incredibly precise reasoned out, spreadsheet-backed, financial model thing about how we could do some for pay lifelong learning things with careful analysis.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}委员会的报告是一份极其精确、 经过推敲、有电子表格支撑的财务模型，说明我们如何做一些付费的终身学习项目，分析得很仔细。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:44.780" end="01:11:47.530" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And then at the end, there was about two pages.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后在报告的末尾，大约有两页纸的篇幅。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:47.530" end="01:11:49.180" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It said, and by the way, we have this other idea that we should just give it away.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}它说，顺便提一下，我们还有另一个想法， 我们应该干脆把这些免费。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:50.830" end="01:11:52.620" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And we'll call it OpenCourseWare.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们会叫它 OpenCourseWare。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:52.620" end="01:11:54.770" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}With no analysis or anything.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}没有任何分析之类的东西。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:11:54.770" end="01:12:00.680" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And then to its tremendous credit, Chuck Bastian, Bob and Tom Magnanti got inspired by this and said yeah, this one seems right.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}接着，极为难能可贵的是，Chuck Bastian（注：此处原文或为 Chuck Vest）、 Bob 和 Tom Magnanti 受此启发，说，对， 这个看上去靠谱。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:12:05.230" end="01:12:09.210" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And that's what actually started the path towards OpenCourseWare.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这就是 OpenCourseWare 之路的起点。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:12:10.870" end="01:12:13.690" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And then there were a lot of talks with--{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后我们进行了很多沟通——{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:12:13.690" end="01:12:15.570" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Chuck went and got money from the Hewlett and Mellon foundations.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}Chuck 到 Hewlett 基金会和 Mellon 基金会那里筹到了资金。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:12:16.940" end="01:12:18.820" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And we did a bunch of things, talked with the faculty over the year.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们也做了一系列的事情， 在这一年里与教师们沟通。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:12:20.230" end="01:12:22.810" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But that's kind of how it started.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但事情大致就是这样开始的。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:12:22.810" end="01:12:27.540" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And again, it started in this world of MIT is going to be the exemplar.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}再说一次，它始于这样一种世界观： MIT 要树立一个榜样。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:12:29.480" end="01:12:33.690" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So we weren't talking really about distance education.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以我们当时谈论的其实并不是远程教育。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:12:33.690" end="01:12:36.203" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We weren't even thinking about the students who were going to do it.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们甚至不是在为那些将要使用它的学生考虑什么。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我得说，主要的负面反应是， 天哪，你们要把我的课堂讲义拿到互联网上让所有人都看到。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们做了一些调整，我们在讲述故事的方式和具体做法上做了一些微调。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}刚才说了，在 2000 年左右， 确实存在一个问题说，互联网上是否能够有大量免费的教育材料。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}那确实曾是个问题。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:18:00.020" end="01:18:01.570" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Now it's not.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}现在已经不是了。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:23:40.530" end="01:23:43.680" >}}

{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We were absolutely right about that.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们对此的判断完全正确。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}很多时候，当人们谈论“开放获取”时，他们会说，哎呀，我应该能够在互联网上读到一些东西，或者做到一些事情，结果它被锁起来了， 我不应该付费才能拿到它。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}它的灵魂在于我们可以共同创造一个共享的东西。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:06.100" end="01:35:10.800" >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我某种程度上把信息环境看作是建造那种大教堂的机会。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:14.080" end="01:35:20.170" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}That humanity as a whole gets smarter because we can rebuild what each others are doing.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}人类作为一个整体会变得更加聪明，因为我们能够重建彼此正在做的事情。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:22.170" end="01:35:24.430" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So that's for me, what open access is about.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以对我来说，这就是“开放获取”的意义所在。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:24.430" end="01:35:25.730" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}That's what OpenCourseWare is about.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这也是 OpenCourseWare 的意义所在。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:25.730" end="01:35:30.280" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So it's critical if you look at the license behind OpenCourseWare or free software, any of it.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以有一点至关重要，如果你去看 OpenCourseWare 或者自由软件背后的许可协议，无论哪一个。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:35.490" end="01:35:40.130" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}One of it is that people get to use it how they want.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}其中一点是，人们可以按照自己的意愿去使用它。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:40.130" end="01:35:45.440" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But the other is that people get to modify and we republish it and make it better and improve.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但另一个是人们可以修改它，重新发布它， 让它变得更好，改进它。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:48.480" end="01:35:50.980" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So for me that's just central to what people call open access.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}对我来说，这就是人们所谓的 “开放获取”的核心。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:35:52.030" end="01:35:59.480" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Open access is in some sense a bad word because it doesn't have this sense of building on each other's work.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}从某种意义上说，“开放获取”这个词取得不好， 因为它没有体现出在彼此工作基础上创造的含义。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:01.610" end="01:36:04.470" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}I'm sort of playing with this new slogan that I want to call the remixed university.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我最近在琢磨一个新口号，我想称之为 “重混大学”（remixed university）。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:07.450" end="01:36:09.520" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}That's the stage after just the open university.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}那是在简单的“开放大学”之后的阶段。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:09.520" end="01:36:10.800" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It's not so interesting.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}后者并没那么有趣。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:10.800" end="01:36:14.300" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}I can go look at the classes that MIT teaches.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我是可以去看 MIT 开设的课程。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:14.300" end="01:36:17.660" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It's can that be a thing from which I can build even better stuff than MIT is doing.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}有趣之处在于，有没有可能让我以此为基础创造出来比 MIT 在做的还要好的东西。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:19.870" end="01:36:25.150" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And that to me is just a central meme in how I hope the internet continues to go.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}对我来说，这是一个核心理念，我希望互联网能按它来继续发展。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:26.560" end="01:36:28.900" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}The internet started a lot of that.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}互联网开创了很多这方面的事物。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Much of it's being threatened.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}其中很大一部分正受到威胁。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:30.160" end="01:36:33.477" >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我认为，这项工作里有一部分工作就是向人们展示这个理念的价值。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:36.150" end="01:36:40.110" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}INTERVIEWER: So in talking or thinking a bit about your work in protecting the intellectual commons, you mentioned the Free Software Foundation, which is definitely something that I wanted to talk to you about.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}采访者：所以，在谈论或思考你在保护知识共享方面的工作时，你提到了自由软件基金会，这肯定是我想和你聊的话题。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}ABELSON: Right.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}ABELSON: 没错。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:36:56.530" end="01:37:01.000" >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}有那么神奇的几年，我们启动了 DSpace， 启动了 OpenCourseWare，展示了 Creative Commons， 大约在 2000 年左右。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:37:10.160" end="01:37:14.630" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So I had the tremendous fortune of actually working with Larry Lessig.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我非常幸运能够与 Larry Lessig 共事。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:37:15.320" end="01:37:19.090" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We tried a joint course between Harvard and MIT when he was formulating these ideas about open culture and things.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}当他正在构思一些关于开放文化等事物的想法时， 我们曾尝试在哈佛大学和 MIT 之间开设一门联合课程。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:37:23.340" end="01:37:28.210" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And Creative Commons kind of started in a couple of discussions, the sense of should there be something about sharing and commons that could happen in terms of law or policy?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}Creative Commons 算是始于几次讨论，关于是否应该在法律或政策方面做一些关于共享和公共领域的事情？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:37:36.550" end="01:37:39.910" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Larry had just recently unsuccessfully argued Eldred v. Ashcroft before the Supreme Court.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}Larry 当时刚刚在最高法院就 Eldred 诉 Ashcroft 案辩论失败。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:37:47.540" end="01:37:50.680" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So that was when Congress extended copyright by another 20 years.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}那是国会将版权期限又延长了 20 年的时候。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:37:52.135" end="01:37:53.850" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And that came up to the Supreme Court.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}那件案子上诉到了最高法院。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:37:53.850" end="01:37:59.380" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And Larry argued at the Supreme Court and he lost.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}Larry 在最高法院进行了辩论，但输了。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:37:59.380" end="01:38:02.250" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}The Supreme Court basically said well, you may have shown that this is a bad idea to extend copyright.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}最高法院基本上说，你或许证明了延长版权是个坏主意。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:04.020" end="01:38:05.530" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But by the way, it's Congress that makes the copyright law, not us.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但顺便一说，制定版权法的是国会，不是我们。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:07.270" end="01:38:13.460" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And Larry was looking for some constructive reaction to that.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}Larry 当时正在对此寻找一些有建设性的回应。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:13.460" end="01:38:18.550" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}I was thinking about some kind of way of rewarding people effectively for putting things into the public domain.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我当时在思考一种方式，从实质上来回报那些将作品放入公共领域的人。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:21.170" end="01:38:25.240" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}What could you do by policy to stimulate that kind of sharing?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}在政策层面，你可以做些什么来激发这种共享？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:26.320" end="01:38:27.570" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We talked about that.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们讨论了这个问题。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:27.570" end="01:38:30.340" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Larry found some funding.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}Larry 找到了一些资金。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:31.810" end="01:38:35.370" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And we got this idea of Creative Commons.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}于是我们有了 Creative Commons 这个想法。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:35.370" end="01:38:37.710" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}There were small group of about, I want to say about 10 of us.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们有个小团队，大约有十个人左右吧。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:40.520" end="01:38:45.280" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And sort of said gee, what we want to do is in the phrase, brand the public domain.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们说，哎呀，我们想做的事情，用一句话概括，就是 “为公共领域打造品牌”。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:47.530" end="01:38:51.410" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}We wanted people to be aware that the shared stuff that you can use and reuse was not sort of the detritus.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们希望人们意识到，那些你可以使用和重用的共享资源并不是某种废弃物。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:56.080" end="01:38:58.990" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}The law in the US talks about abandoning something to the public domain.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}美国法律谈到将某物"遗弃"给公共领域。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:38:59.910" end="01:39:02.310" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It was not sort of this invisible stuff.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}它不是这种没人注意的东西。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:02.310" end="01:39:04.790" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}One of the things you can do on the internet is you can actually give that an identity and make people aware of it.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}在互联网上你能做的一件事是，你可以给它一个身份，让人们意识到它的存在。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:08.910" end="01:39:11.530" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}That was the soul of Creative Commons.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}那才是 Creative Commons 的灵魂。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:11.530" end="01:39:15.290" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And then it kind of linked into some stuff that I'd been doing with the Web Consortium that said oh by the way, one of the things you might want to do if you're going to make licenses crafted to that, you want to make those licenses machine readable so machines can identify that on the internet.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后它又和我与万维网联盟（WebConsortium） 合作的事情联系起来， 说顺便一提，如果你要为这个目的设计许可协议，你可能会想让机器能读取这些许可， 以便机器能在互联网上识别它们。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:31.120" end="01:39:32.550" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So that's the start of Creative Commons.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这就是 Creative Commons 的起点。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:32.550" end="01:39:34.830" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And that program is sort of still going ahead.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这个项目目前仍在继续前进。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:34.830" end="01:39:36.340" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It's got a long, long, long way to go.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}它还有很长、很长、很长的路要走。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:36.340" end="01:39:40.490" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}I remember we were sitting around and saying well, what would be success?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我记得我们曾坐在一起讨论说， 怎样才算是成功了？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}How many things do you think should have these licenses?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}你认为有多少东西应该采用这些许可协议？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So I'm always the poor non-visionary.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Right.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}对。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:54.490" end="01:39:57.530" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And I said, gosh if we got a couple of million of things on the net with the Creative Commons, that would be really good.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我说，天哪，如果网络能有数百万个采用 Creative Commons 的东西， 那就真的很不错了。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:39:59.820" end="01:40:02.520" >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}而 Larry 则说，我其实认为所有内容都应该采用 Creative Commons。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And then we seem to have compromised.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后我们似乎折中了一下。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:40:06.220" end="01:40:09.540" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Now there's about 200 million Creative Commons documents on the net.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}现在网上大约有 2 亿份采用 Creative Commons 的文档。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:40:11.130" end="01:40:13.310" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So it will also hit a meme and expand it.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以它也会成为一个热门的理念，然后扩展它。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:40:13.310" end="01:40:16.840" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And by the way, had a lot to do with OpenCourseWare.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}顺便说一下，这与 OpenCourseWare 有很大关系。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So I was very active in the start up of both of those.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我在这两者的创立过程中都非常活跃。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:40:22.690" end="01:40:28.340" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And from the point of view of Creative Commons, MIT was the first sort of big, important place to adopt Creative Commons licenses.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}从 Creative Commons 的角度看， MIT 是第一个采用 Creative Commons 许可的重要机构。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:40:34.140" end="01:40:38.520" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And from the point of view of OpenCourseWare, we wanted there to be a lot of freely licensed stuff on the web.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}而从 OpenCourseWare 的角度看，我们希望网络上有大量自由许可的资源。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:40:42.760" end="01:40:49.300" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So in particular when I put up my lectures on OpenCourseWare and I want to put some illustrations into my lecture, there's a lot of Creative Commons licensed stuff that I could just use.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}特别是当我把自己的讲座放到 OpenCourseWare 上， 并且想在讲义中加入一些插图时，我有大量采用 Creative Commons 许可的资源可以直接使用。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:40:55.350" end="01:40:58.895" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So that program still hasn't unfolded a lot.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}所以这个项目还没有完全展开。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:40:58.895" end="01:41:00.010" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But it was very consciously--{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但它是非常有意识地——{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:48:55.025" end="01:48:59.730" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}Are there ways we can translate little pieces of MIT so that MIT students can have some of these experiences without feeling that they have to blow off courses for a semester?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}是否有办法转化 MIT 的一小部分， 让 MIT 的学生能够获得这些体验， 而不用觉得他们必须水掉一整个学期的课？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:49:10.040" end="01:49:12.370" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}The mechanical engineering department talks about wouldn't it be great if students in mechanical engineering could take two weeks off and go build cars and race them on the Isle of White.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}机械工程系在讨论，如果机械工程的学生能休假两周， 去怀特岛造车并拿它们赛车， 那该多好。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:49:21.000" end="01:49:24.400" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}How do we make that possible?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们如何使之成为可能？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:49:24.400" end="01:49:29.580" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So that's a direction where I think MIT needs to go.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这是我认为 MIT 应当前进的一个方向。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:49:29.580" end="01:49:33.370" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}I said there's this buzz word, the remixed university.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我刚才提到了一个流行词，"重混大学"。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:49:33.370" end="01:49:36.870" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}How do we make that possible and how does MIT lead in showing how you can make that possible?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们如何实现它，MIT 又如何在展示这种可能性方面发挥领导作用？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:49:38.310" end="01:49:41.940" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}INTERVIEWER: I mean MIT obviously is a place with tremendous technical technological expertise.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}采访者：我想说，MIT 显然是一个拥有强大技术专长的地方。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:49:48.440" end="01:49:51.030" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But our conversation has ranged over all sorts of topics that go beyond simple technology, policy issues, just how we live our lives in the world.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但我们的谈话涉及了各种各样的话题， 超越了单纯的技术、政策问题，触及到我们在世界上如何生活。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:49:57.690" end="01:50:02.560" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And I'm wondering if you could talk a bit about what special or particular role technologists, engineers should or could play in those broader ethical, philosophical, policy kinds of questions?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我在想，能否谈谈什么特殊或者特定的角色， 是技术人员、工程师在这些更广泛的伦理、哲学、政策类问题中， 应该或能够扮演的？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:50:13.510" end="01:50:17.540" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}ABELSON: Well, part is the easy thing about just knowing the consequences or the likely consequences of certain kinds of investments or policies.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}ABELSON：嗯，一部分是比较容易的事情，比如知晓某些投资或政策的后果或可能的后果。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:50:28.580" end="01:50:33.170" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And I don't think anybody will argue that engineers and scientists should speak up about that.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我想不会有人反对，工程师和科学家应当就这些问题发声。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:50:37.360" end="01:50:41.960" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But I think beyond that there's this sense of actually making things, which I do think is very special to engineering.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但我认为在此之上，还有一种"真正去创造东西"的意识，我确实认为这是工程领域的独特之处。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:50:47.220" end="01:50:51.110" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It's really find to talk about things and to discuss, and discuss, and discuss, but at the end of the day you have to have some effect and some kind of impact.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}谈论事情，讨论、讨论再讨论，当然很好，但归根结底，你必须要有一些实际效果，产生一些影响。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:01.720" end="01:51:06.380" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And engineers are great in doing things.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}而工程师们很擅长实际行动。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:06.380" end="01:51:08.650" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It's not always right.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}结果未必总是对的。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:08.650" end="01:51:12.410" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But there's this notion of you kind of have to put it on the line and make something.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但有一种观念是，你必须承担风险， 做出一点东西来。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:15.330" end="01:51:21.550" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And that's part of what it means to, I want to say participate in the discussion of how the world should be.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我想说，参与“世界应该是什么样子”的讨论，就带着得去这样做的意味。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:24.350" end="01:51:27.190" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}You come in and you actually think about how to make it.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}你加入进来，你真正去思考如何实现它。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:27.190" end="01:51:27.680" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And you try it.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后你去尝试。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:27.680" end="01:51:29.090" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And you never get it right the first time.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}你永远不会一次就做对。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:29.090" end="01:51:30.660" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And then you make it better.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}然后你把它做得更好。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:30.660" end="01:51:37.150" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And there needs to be that sense of instrumentality.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}这其中需要有一种工具性的意识。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:37.150" end="01:51:39.330" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And that's what I think a place like MIT and a place like engineering cultures can add to these discussions.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我认为这正是像 MIT 这样的地方， 以及工程文化，能够为这些讨论增添的东西。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:42.850" end="01:51:46.070" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And there needs to be a whole lot more of that.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我们需要更多大量这样的东西。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:46.070" end="01:51:47.620" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}INTERVIEWER: Is there anything that you haven't had a chance to talk about that we should have touched on as we're wrapping up.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}采访者：在我们即将结束之际，有没有什么你还没机会谈到，但我们本应该触及的话题？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:51:55.690" end="01:52:05.270" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}ABELSON: Well no, other than I'm constantly humbled and amazed and charged by just the privilege of being in a place like MIT.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}ABELSON：嗯，没有了，除了我始终对自己能有幸身处 MIT 这样的地方感到受宠若惊，它如此惊艳， 让我充满动力。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:09.730" end="01:52:13.030" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}I mean everybody talks about what a unique place it is.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我的意思是，大家都说这是一个多么独特的地方。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:13.030" end="01:52:17.220" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}But there's just this personal sense of how in hell did I ever end up here, interacting with this group of people?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}但我个人总有一种感觉，我到底是怎么能来到这里，与这群人共事的？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:20.660" end="01:52:23.180" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}So I drive in from Newton every morning.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我每天早上从 Newton 开车过来。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:23.180" end="01:52:25.475" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And there's this place where you drive up Commonwealth Avenue and then you sort of turn and go over the BU Bridge.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}有一个地方，你沿着联邦大道开车， 然后你转弯，开过波士顿大学桥。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:29.595" end="01:52:31.640" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And the BU Bridge sort of looks like this gateway thing.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}波士顿大学桥看起来就像是一个大门。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:31.640" end="01:52:34.300" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}And I say, I can't believe it.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我会说，我简直不敢相信。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:34.300" end="01:52:37.525" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}It's almost every day, after so many years, I say oh my god, I'm coming to MIT.{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}几乎每天，这么多年了，我都会说，老天爷， 我要去 MIT 了。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< /track-segment >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:41.360" end="01:52:43.790" >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-en" >}}How did I manage to do this?{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我是怎么做到的？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< track-segment start="01:52:43.790" end="01:52:48.350" >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}我是何其有幸能身处这样一个地方， 周围全是这些才华横溢的人， 这些出类拔萃的学生？{{< /styled-paragraph >}}

{{< styled-paragraph class="lang-cn" >}}采访者：好的。{{< /styled-paragraph >}}
